If there is a higher-end twin room, I will definitely choose a higher-end one, but unfortunately there is none. The room faces Badaguan and can see a little sea. The room faces northwest. The comments of the same room type can face the southeast and see the coast, which may be a free upgrade. The TV is quite large, but it cannot be projected, and there is no network TV, which is not good. There is less lighting in the room. The glass is a little dirty, but you can see the scenery clearly. There is no bathtub, and the water will suddenly heat up after turning off. The room type is relatively small, the bed is also relatively small, there is no sofa with a backrest, only one without a backrest, and you can't sit for a long time. The room is relatively hot, but the air conditioner seems to be unable to cool at present. The fitness center is very high-end, but some employees are impatient and have a bad attitude, and the location of the swimming pool is more difficult. The hotel staff has a good attitude and can effectively solve the problems encountered during check-in. However, I experienced a situation where the hotel did not have disposable chopsticks, and no tableware could be borrowed. This can be improved. Because the hotel's overall service is good, it gave a good review.

The room service surprised me a bit. The cleaning aunt was very polite. Seeing that my child was sleeping on the sofa in the living room, she carefully wrapped the sofa with sheets. . Finally, the geographical location, relying on the third seaside bathing beach, there is a beach opposite to the downstairs, a few steps to the west is Taipingjiao Park, and Badaguan passes through it. I like this location very much. Compared with the Vientiane City area where I lived before the trip to Qingdao, it looks elegant and less crowded. Although the scale of the hotel is not very large, and there is a confinement center downstairs, it still makes me very satisfied. Next time I go to Qingdao, I will choose Haiyi.
